 faceapp - is an app that is becoming quite popular in India these days
 news feed main aisi photose kii bharmaar he jisamen log buudhe dikh rahe hai
 This app is not new, it is already
 lekin bharat main aaj kal ye trend main he
 Actually, this app has many features, one of which is to make the face look old
 faceapp ke mutabik company artificial intelligence technolji kaa yuj karke aisa karti he
 This app was launched in 2017
 kya ise yuj karne main risk he? kya ye aapke photo libraci kaa phul acces letaa he? is tarah ke sawaal logon ke man main uth rahe hai
 This app is using not only common users but now celebrity and due to this it is getting more hype
 photose ko edit karne ke liye ye ap neural network yuj karata he
 Neural networks are a type of artificial intelligence
 na sirf aij balki is ap se yangar luk, gender swap jaise task bhi kiye ja sakate hai
 What does the privacy policy of faceapp say? Whenever you use our service, our service automatically records some log file information
 inamen aapkaa web request, ypi adress, broujar tip, yuarel or aap is sarvice ke saath kitni baar interact karte hai is tarah kii jaankaree shaamil he
 It has also been said in the policy that the company will not sell user data without their permission and will not rent to anyone
 haalanki phase ap ke group kii companiyon ko aapkaa data diya ja saktaa he, kyonki aapane iske concent diya he
 According to the company's policy, if the company wants, then the third party can provide some information to the advertising partners
 inamen kukaj data shaamil hai

 haalanki security research Robert Baptiste ke mutabik aisa nahin he or iskaa koi pramaan nahin mila he
 But obviously you are giving 100% permission to the photo you are editing

 twitter

 unhone sawaal uthaaya he ki bina parmishan ke ye ap photo kaise le saktaa he
